***жавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жавший.html>жа́вший</a> (7091)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жавший.html>жа́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žávšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***жадный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жадный.html>жа́дный</a> (5930)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">жадьнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žadĭnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žędьnъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">avid, greedy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жадный.html>жа́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žádnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)жадне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)жадне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>greedy</li>
<li>avaricious, covetous <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + dative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>selfish</li></ol>

***жажда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жажда.html>жа́жда</a> (3760)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">жѩжда</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žjęžda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žęďa</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žędati</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ja</i>. Displaced native <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">жажа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žaža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жажда.html>жа́жда</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žážda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жажда.html>жа́жды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жажда.html>жа́жды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жажда.html>жа́жд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>thirst</li>
<li>craving
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:жажда.html>жа́жда</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:знание.html>зна́ний</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">žážda znánij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">thirst for knowledge, hunger for knowledge</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:жажда.html>жа́жда</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровь.html>крови</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">žážda krovi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blood lust</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жаждать.html>жа́ждать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žáždatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

***жаждущий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жаждущий.html>жа́ждущий</a> (5762)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жаждущий.html>жа́ждущий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žážduščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жаждать.html>жа́ждать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žáždatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жаждущий.html>жа́ждущий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žážduščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>thirsty, avid, desirous, ambitious</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The term is not used to express "to be thirsty". To say "I'm thirsty", use "<a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хочу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пить</a>" or "<a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеться.html>хо́чется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пить</a>", literally: I want to drink.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жалеть.html>жале́ть</a> (1633)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жалеть.html>жале́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žalétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожалеть.html>пожале́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to feel sorry, to be sorry, to be sad (about something), to regret</li>
<li>to pity, to commiserate</li>
<li>to save, to spare (e.g. time, energy)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жалоба.html>жа́лоба</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">žáloba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жалость.html>жа́лость</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">žálostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожалеть.html>сожале́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sožalétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***жалкий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жалкий.html>жа́лкий</a> (2444)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жалкий.html>жа́лкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žálkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)жа́льче</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)жа́лче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pitiable</li>
<li>miserable, pitiful, wretched
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can we date this quote?)</span>,  Evgeny Shvarts,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:тень.html>Тень</a></cite>  | <cite>Shadow</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жете</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любой.html>любо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>само́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жалкий.html>жа́лкой</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поза.html>по́зе</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Móžete stojátʹ v ljubój samój <b>žálkoj</b> póze.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You can stand at any position most <b>miserable</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>pathetic
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> жа́льче <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On dáže i žálʹče menjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is even more pitiful than I.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жалко.html>жа́лко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žálko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>pitiably, miserably, wretchedly</li>
<li>negligibly</li>
<li>plaintively</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жалкий.html>жа́лкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žálkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>sorry, it is a pity</li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жа́ло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žálo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жа́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жа́ла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жал</a></b>)

***жалованье.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жалованье.html>жа́лованье</a> (10255)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жалованье.html>жа́лованье</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žálovanʹje</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жалованье.html>жа́лованья</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жалованье.html>жа́лованья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жалованье.html>жа́лований</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pay, salary; wages; stipend</li></ol>

***жаловать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жаловать.html>жа́ловать</a> (12186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жаловать.html>жа́ловать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žálovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожаловать.html>пожа́ловать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grant, to bestow, to confer, to reward, to award <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">stilted style</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to favour, to regard with favour; to like
<dl><dd><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> о́чень-то <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жаловать.html>жа́луют</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jevó ne óčenʹ-to <b>žálujut</b> tam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is not very <a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a> there.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:просить.html>прошу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жаловать.html>жа́ловать</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prošú ljubítʹ i <b>žálovatʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">please welcome; I would like you to welcome <i>(oneself or somebody who is introduced)</i></span></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to visit, to come to see <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">stilted style or jocular</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жалость.html>жа́лость</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žálostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ливый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-livyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***жалюзи.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жалюзи.html>жалюзи́</a> (19750)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">jalousie</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жалюзи.html>жалюзи́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žaljuzí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>blind, jalousie</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The accent pattern "<a href = vnd.unilang:жалюзи.html>жа́люзи</a>" is non-standard.</li>
<li>The term is officially neuter singular and indeclinable but it can be declinable and plural in non-standard Russian.</li></ul>

***жар.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жар.html>жар</a> (2171)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žarъ</i>. See also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греть.html>греть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gretʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жар.html>жар</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žar</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жар.html>жа́ра</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>heat</li>
<li>ardour</li>
<li>fever, high temperature</li>
<li>embers</li></ol>

***жара.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жар.html>жара</a> (6327)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žārь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʷher-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to heat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi">Hindi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">गर्म</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">garma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi">Hindi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">गर्मी</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">garmī</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language">Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq">zjarr</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Armenian" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Armenian">Old Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="xcl">ջեր</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xcl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ǰer</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fornāx</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">varmr</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Prussian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Prussian language">Old Prussian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="prg">goro</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hearth; stove</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
